  <script type="text/javascript">
      //<![CDATA[
      function removeHtmlTag(strx,chop){ 
        if(strx.indexOf("<")!=-1)
        {
          var s = strx.split("<"); 
          for(var i=0;i<s.length;i++){ 
            if(s[i].indexOf(">")!=-1){ 
              s[i] = s[i].substring(s[i].indexOf(">")+1,s[i].length); 
            } 
          } 
          strx =  s.join(""); 
        }
        chop = (chop < strx.length-1) ? chop : strx.length-2; 
        while(strx.charAt(chop-1)!=' ' && strx.indexOf(' ',chop)!=-1) chop++; 
        strx = strx.substring(0,chop-1); 
        return strx+'...'; 
      }
      function createSummaryAndThumb(pID){
        var div = document.getElementById(pID);
        var imgtag = "";
        var img = div.getElementsByTagName("img");
        var summ = summary_noimg;
        if(img.length>=1) {	
          imgtag = '<img src="'+img[0].src+'" class="pbtthumbimg"/>';
          summ = summary_img;
        }
        var summary = imgtag + '<div>' + removeHtmlTag(div.innerHTML,summ) + '</div>';
        div.innerHTML = summary;
      }

      }

    (function() {
      var gwdAd = document.getElementById('gwd-ad');

      /**
       * Handles the DOMContentLoaded event. The DOMContentLoaded event is
       * fired when the document has been completely loaded and parsed.
       */
      function handleDomContentLoaded(event) {

      }

      /**
       * Handles the WebComponentsReady event. This event is fired when all
       * custom elements have been registered and upgraded.
       */
      function handleWebComponentsReady(event) {
        // Start the Ad lifecycle.
        setTimeout(function() {
          gwdAd.initAd();
        }, 0);
      }

      /**
       * Handles the event that is dispatched after the Ad has been
       * initialized and before the default page of the Ad is shown.
       */
      function handleAdInitialized(event) {}

      window.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded',
        handleDomContentLoaded, false);
      window.addEventListener('WebComponentsReady',
        handleWebComponentsReady, false);
      window.addEventListener('adinitialized',
        handleAdInitialized, false);
    })();

                <b><u><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%;"><br></span></u></b>

                <span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-no-proof: yes;">

                <span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%;">
                 <o:p></o:p></span>
               </div> 
               <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"> 
                <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-oBaHi02Sl_c/Urz96QMweqI/AAAAAAAAFIA/fHc9vBlAuBY/s1600/Capture.PNG" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;"><img border="0" height="275" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-oBaHi02Sl_c/Urz96QMweqI/AAAAAAAAFIA/fHc9vBlAuBY/s1600/Capture.PNG" width="400"></a>
               </div> 
               <div class="MsoNormal"> 
                <b><u><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-themecolor: text1; mso-themetint: 217;"><br></span></u></b>
               </div> 
               <div class="MsoNormal"> 
                <b><u><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-themecolor: text1; mso-themetint: 217;"><br></span></u></b>
               </div> 
               <div class="MsoNormal"> 
                <b><u><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-themecolor: text1; mso-themetint: 217;">Procedure for deploy portlet:
                   <o:p></o:p></span></u></b>
               </div> 
               <div class="MsoNormal"> 
                <b><u><span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-themecolor: text1; mso-themetint: 217;"><br></span></u></b>
               </div> 
               <div class="MsoNormal"> 
                <span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-themecolor: text1; mso-themetint: 217;">You can use war file and directly place in your portal deploy folder and test or you can also use source to deploy portlet.
                 <o:p></o:p></span>
               </div> 
               <div class="MsoNormal"> 
                <span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-themecolor: text1; mso-themetint: 217;"><br></span>
               </div> 
               <div class="MsoNormal"> 
                <span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-themecolor: text1; mso-themetint: 217;">Once portlet is deployed successfully you can see the portlet in sample category name as <b>Liferay Captcha Action</b></span>
                <span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%;">
                 <o:p></o:p></span>
               </div> 
               <div class="MsoNormal"> 
                <span style="color: #262626; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%; mso-themecolor: text1; mso-themetint: 217;"><b><br></b></span>
               </div> 
               <div class="MsoNormal"> 
                <span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%;">Some time we need captcha to submit forms in liferay portlet development. Liferay already have captcha generated library from which we can generate captcha and verify the captcha.
                 <o:p></o:p></span>
               </div> 
               <div class="MsoNormal"> 
                <span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%;"><br></span>
               </div> 
               <div class="MsoNormal"> 
                <span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%;">Liferay have inbuilt tag library to display captcha in JSP page. And liferay captcha tag needs URL as parameter form that it will get captcha image.
                 <o:p></o:p></span>
               </div> 
               <div class="MsoNormal"> 
                <span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%;"><br></span>
               </div> 
               <div class="MsoNormal"> 
                <span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%;">Liferay have one of the java class called <b><i>CaptchaUtil</i></b> so that we can generate image and we can verify the captcha image.
                 <o:p></o:p></span>
               </div> 
               <div class="MsoNormal"> 
                <span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%;"><br></span>
               </div> 
               <div class="MsoNormal"> 
                <span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%;">The following are the two methods which we use in the portlet
                 <o:p></o:p></span>
               </div> 
               <div class="MsoNormal"> 
                <span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%;"><br></span>
               </div> 
               <div class="MsoNormal"> 
                <b><i><u><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%;">serveImage</span></u></i></b>
                <u><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%;"> method to generate captcha Image
                  <o:p></o:p></span></u>
               </div> 
               <div class="MsoNormal"> 
                <u><span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt; line-height: 115%;"><br></span></u>
               </div>

                     <o:p></o:p></span>

                    <span style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 13pt;">CaptchaUtil.<i>serveImage</i>(resourceRequest, resourceResponse);</span>
                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div>

                    <span style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 13pt;">}</span>

                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div> 
                   <div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;">

                    <span style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 13pt;">.error(e);</span>
                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div> 
                   <div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;"> 
                    <span style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 13pt;">}</span>

                     <o:p></o:p></span>

                     <o:p></o:p></span>

                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 13.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>

                     <o:p></o:p></span>

                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div> 
                   <div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;"> 
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; System.</span>
                    <i><span style="color: #0000c0; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">out</span></i>
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">.println(</span>
                    <span style="color: #2a00ff; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">"firstName::"</span>
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">+firstName);</span>
                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div> 
                   <div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;"> 
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; System.</span>
                    <i><span style="color: #0000c0; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">out</span></i>
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">.println(</span>
                    <span style="color: #2a00ff; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">"lastName::"</span>
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">+lastName);</span>
                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div> 
                   <div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;"> 
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>
                    <b><span style="color: #7f0055; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">try</span></b>
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">{</span>
                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div> 
                   <div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;"> 
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; CaptchaUtil.<i>check</i>(actionRequest);</span>
                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div> 
                   <div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;"> 
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }</span>
                    <b><span style="color: #7f0055; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">catch</span></b>
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">(Exception e){</span>
                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div> 
                   <div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;"> 
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>
                    <b><span style="color: #7f0055; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">if</span></b>
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;"> (e </span>
                    <b><span style="color: #7f0055; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">instanceof</span></b>
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;"> CaptchaTextException || e </span>
                    <b><span style="color: #7f0055; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">instanceof</span></b>
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;"> CaptchaMaxChallengesException ){</span>
                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div> 
                   <div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;"> 
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; SessionErrors.<i>add</i>(actionRequest, e.getClass(), e);</span>
                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div> 
                   <div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;"> 
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>
                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div> 
                   <div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;"> 
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }</span>
                    <b><span style="color: #7f0055; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">else</span></b>
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">{</span>
                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div> 
                   <div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;"> 
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; System.</span>
                    <i><span style="color: #0000c0; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">out</span></i>
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">.println(</span>
                    <span style="color: #2a00ff; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">"Captcha verification success::"</span>
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">);</span>
                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div> 
                   <div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;"> 
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }</span>
                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div> 
                   <div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;"> 
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>
                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div>

                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }</span>
                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div> 
                   <div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;"> 
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>
                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div>

                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; }</span>

                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div> 
                   <div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;"> 
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>

                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div> 
                   <div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;"> 
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>
                    <span style="color: #646464; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">@Override</span>
                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div> 
                   <div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;"> 
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>
                    <b><span style="color: #7f0055; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">public</span></b>
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;"> </span>
                    <b><span style="color: #7f0055; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">void</span></b>
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;"> serveResource(ResourceRequest resourceRequest,</span>
                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div> 
                   <div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;"> 
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; ResourceResponse resourceResponse)</span>
                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div> 
                   <div class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;"> 
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>
                    <b><span style="color: #7f0055; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">throws</span></b>
                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp; IOException, PortletException {</span>
                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>
                   </div>

                    <br>
                   </div>

                     <o:p></o:p></span>

                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; CaptchaUtil.<i>serveImage</i>(resourceRequest, resourceResponse);</span>
                    <span style="font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">
                     <o:p></o:p></span>

                     <o:p></o:p></span>

                     <o:p></o:p></span>

                    <i><span style="color: #0000c0; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">_CHECK_METHOD_ON_PROCESS_ACTION</span></i>

                    <span style="font-family: 'Courier New'; font-size: 10pt;"> = </span>
                    <b><span style="color: #7f0055; font-family: &quot;Courier New&quot;; font-size: 10.0pt;">false</span></b>

    window.followersIframe = null;
    function followersIframeOpen(url) {
      gapi.load("gapi.iframes", function() {
        if (gapi.iframes && gapi.iframes.getContext) {
          window.followersIframe = gapi.iframes.getContext().openChild({
            url: url,
            where: document.getElementById("followers-iframe-container"),
            messageHandlersFilter: gapi.iframes.CROSS_ORIGIN_IFRAMES_FILTER,
            messageHandlers: {
              '_ready': function(obj) {
                window.followersIframe.getIframeEl().height = obj.height;
              },
              'reset': function() {
                window.followersIframe.close();
                followersIframeOpen("https://www.blogger.com/followers.g?blogID\x3d4305105234376370815\x26colors\x3dCgt0cmFuc3BhcmVudBILdHJhbnNwYXJlbnQaByMwMDAwMDAiByMwMDAwMDAqByNGRkZGRkYyByMwMDAwMDA6ByMwMDAwMDBCByMwMDAwMDBKByMwMDAwMDBSByNGRkZGRkZaC3RyYW5zcGFyZW50\x26pageSize\x3d21\x26postID\x3d2030980661412222023\x26origin\x3dhttp://www.liferaysavvy.com/");
              },
              'open': function(url) {
                window.followersIframe.close();
                followersIframeOpen(url);
              },
              'blogger-ping': function() {
              }
            }
          });
        }
      });
    }

  <script type="text/javascript">
      //<![CDATA[
      /**
 * navigation.js
 *
 * Handles toggling the navigation menu for small screens.
 */
      ( function() {
        var container, button, menu;
        container = document.getElementById( 'site-navigationpbt' );
        if ( ! container )
          return;
        button = container.getElementsByTagName( 'h1' )[0];
        if ( 'undefined' === typeof button )
          return;
        menu = container.getElementsByTagName( 'ul' )[0];
        // Hide menu toggle button if menu is empty and return early.
        if ( 'undefined' === typeof menu ) {
          button.style.display = 'none';
          return;
        }
        if ( -1 === menu.className.indexOf( 'nav-menu' ) )
          menu.className += ' nav-menu';
        button.onclick = function() {
          if ( -1 !== container.className.indexOf( 'toggled' ) )
            container.className = container.className.replace( ' toggled', '' );
          else
            container.className += ' toggled';
        };
      } )();
      //]]>
    </script> 
  <script type="text/javascript">
      //<![CDATA[
      ( function() {
        var is_webkit = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().indexOf( 'webkit' ) > -1,
            is_opera  = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().indexOf( 'opera' )  > -1,
            is_ie     = navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase().indexOf( 'msie' )   > -1;
        if ( ( is_webkit || is_opera || is_ie ) && 'undefined' !== typeof( document.getElementById ) ) {
          var eventMethod = ( window.addEventListener ) ? 'addEventListener' : 'attachEvent';
          window[ eventMethod ]( 'hashchange', function() {
            var element = document.getElementById( location.hash.substring( 1 ) );
            if ( element ) {
              if ( ! /^(?:a|select|input|button|textarea)$/i.test( element.tagName ) )
                element.tabIndex = -1;
              element.focus();
            }
          }, false );
        }
      })();
      //]]>
    </script>
